They do not feel pain in this way of life. Because they carry salt out in the morning and sell it all by evening. They use the money they earn to buy rice and fish for their husbands and sons to eat their fill.

However, in recent years, their lives have not been as pleasant as in the past. Because when they carry salt on the streets or on the country roads, shouting: "Do you want salt?" they are often caught and beaten by the water police, who also take away the salt. They are even detained in prison! In this way, the husbands and sons at home are hungry for a whole night.

They now have a passive resistance method to deal with the water police: they often carry salt together in groups of several people, walking on the streets or roads; when they encounter the water police, they unceremoniously use their thick fists and hard carrying poles to beat the water police to near death, retaliating for the previous beatings.

They can also carry out women's movements. They united all the women in Baihu Village and the women who buy salt nearby, and went to the county government to petition, demanding the abolition of the bad practice of catching salt. Their reason is this:

"The salt is produced locally, can't the local people enjoy the salt produced locally?"

But the county government's answer is: "Salt is public property, so it must be sold publicly like opium."

A Treatise on the Causes of Unemployment for Laborers 248

— Songfu

The formation of the unemployment problem is a characteristic of the capitalist social organization. In the handicraft era of the feudal system, although there were occasional special and abnormal events that were enough to affect people's occupations and livelihoods, they were only a small part of the population, and there was no other kind of mutual connection. When capitalism developed, most of the proletarians had to abandon their old occupations and gathered from villages and towns to large factories in the cities to become wage laborers. An accident in a large factory is enough to affect the unemployment of many laborers, and the result of unemployment, needless to say, is the misery of the unemployed laborers themselves. In this way, the unemployment problem of laborers has become an important problem in modern society. Therefore, the biggest reason for promoting the unemployment problem is fundamentally the deformity and unreasonableness of the current social organization. The more developed capitalism is, the more alarming the increase in the number of unemployed people. It can be imagined from the large number of people registered in the employment agencies and those who apply for union subsidies in various capitalist countries.

Shinjiro Kitazawa of Japan divides the social causes of unemployment into: (1) seasonal changes in labor demand, (2) cyclical decline in the industrial world, (3) the existence of temporary day labor systems, and (4) changes in overproduction caused by advances in technology and organization. This classification is more universal and suitable. Now, I will briefly explain the social causes of unemployment in these four aspects as follows:

(1) Seasonal changes in labor demand The difference in the degree of prosperity and slackness of most occupations is dominated by time. The difference in the demand for laborers will cause a shortage or surplus of laborers depending on the season of the industry. When a certain industry is prosperous, there is no problem with the working life of the laborers in that occupation: if the industry declines due to climate, social trends, or the trend of the times, laborers will feel a lack of work and unemployment will occur. Most industries are time-sensitive, so this factor has a great impact on the unemployment problem. This is especially true for skilled laborers, because skilled laborers are limited to certain skilled jobs; other occupations are not their strengths.

(2) Cyclical decline in the industrial world In the past economic history, it is clear that the economic society has traces of cyclical decline, prosperity, and decline. The market is dominated by social, economic, geographical, customs, and other factors, and there are often phenomena of decline and prosperity: and this phenomenon sometimes occurs not only in a part of the space, but also has a mutually related force that is enough to involve the overall situation, such as the successive closures of my country's yarn factories in the past few years. Once the market in the economic society declines, the unemployment situation of laborers is very terrible.

(3) The existence of temporary day labor systems Temporary day laborers can also be said to be unemployed people who get temporary work, which is also an infrequent and accidental thing, because each factory has sufficient long-term contract workers in places that need workers, and there are very few places that need temporary day laborers. These workers do not have fixed long-term occupations, and most of them wait near factories, companies, stations, docks, etc., waiting for someone to hire them. The coolies on the wharves of the Huangpu River in Shanghai are a part of this type of worker.

(4) Changes in overproduction caused by advances in technology and organization The invention of machinery, the advancement of production methods and production systems can reduce the consumption of production and increase the output of products. As a result, the excess of laborers and their skilled skills become unnecessary, and some laborers have to suffer the tragedy of unemployment.

Public News

Impressions of a Reader's Talk at a Certain Library 249

— Wen Xin

The reading room was densely packed with fifty or sixty people, it was difficult to find a dark head, people wearing new clothes - so-called "modern". Then the meeting began!

A burly worker stood up and spoke slowly and in detail, word by word.

A middle school student, his face red, his voice trembling a little.

A shop apprentice reported his early departure to the chairman, his voice so soft that it could not be heard, while touching his nose with his hand.

This group of people who have been deprived of the freedom of assembly and association by factory owners, principals, and managers! They show their weaknesses in the meeting place (although not a large meeting place), but these weaknesses are easy to overcome.

They sat quietly in their seats, earnestly discussing issues, creating an atmosphere of solemnity and solemnity in the room. Behind this solemn and solemn atmosphere, it seemed that they heard the cries of the great souls of the laboring masses? Enough, let those bird meeting rituals and etiquette be thrown into the latrine! We don't need them!

When the chairman announced the adjournment, many people still had a lot to say! - It can be seen from those faces. The time seemed a little short.

Book and Newspaper Chronicles

"How to Study the New Social Sciences" and Others 250

— Xin

Dear readers: Nowadays, many people of your same status, when they have free time, either flip through newspapers to find news such as rape, or talk to others about everything about women. But you are able to use your free time to read this magazine, which I admire very much.

When you see that the "Self-Employment Introduction" column in this magazine is often full, and that even in the United States, which is called the Golden Country, there are millions of unemployed workers; while on the other hand, in a country that occupies one-sixth of the earth - the Soviet Union, not only is there not a single unemployed person, but there is a need for a large number of workers to work, etc., you may wonder about all these phenomena in your heart, but you cannot answer how these phenomena occur. Among you, some have studied in schools, but the teachers will not tell you the reasons for all social phenomena; not to mention those who have not attended school. And what about your bosses or senior brothers? I am afraid that there are very few who can accurately answer these social phenomena; some simply do not know what is going on.

Now let me introduce a book "How to Study the New Social Sciences" (edited by Ke Bonian, published by Nanqiang Bookstore, 35 cents per copy). This book, although it cannot immediately tell you the reasons for all the above-mentioned social phenomena; but it will tell you some methods of studying social phenomena. After reading this book, and then gradually selecting and studying according to the bibliography listed at the back of the book, in this way, not only can you get the answers to all the above-mentioned social phenomena, but also other social problems will be answered, and at the same time, your knowledge will be greatly enriched. There is also a book "Introduction to Social Sciences" (edited by Yang Jianxiu, published by Modern Bookstore, 40 cents per copy). Although some parts of this book are not very accurate, it can be used to know what the meaning of society is, what its structure is, and how politics, law, religion, morality, and art occur.

Also, when you have free time, in addition to reading newspapers, you probably read novels such as "Tears and Laughter Marriage" or "Wild River Heroine", but after reading these novels, what are your feelings? Probably not imagining yourself as an affectionate son, or becoming an expert in all kinds of weapons like in the book? When Japan and all imperialists are actively dividing China, these novels will only make people indulge in that kind of fantasy, and in fact, they are destroying the power of the masses to resist Japan and oppose imperialism. The novels that need to be read now should be suitable for the current situation, so I hope you will read novels with profound meaning such as "Volunteer Army", "Midnight", "Cement", "Iron Flow", "Collapse", "Brosky", etc.

Appendix: If you encounter many new terms when reading books, such as "capitalism", "socialism", "historical materialism", etc., you can refer to the "New Terminology Dictionary"! It should be available in the library of this newspaper!

Letters Published 253

To Mr. Liangcai, Editor:

Respectfully, your newspaper's amateur weekly published on the 2nd and 9th of this month the letter from female worker Zhu Yongli and our factory. We would like to invite Qing. Yesterday, I was afraid that I would not be able to express myself clearly on the phone, so I will extend it as follows: 1. Your newspaper's establishment of a job introduction column to serve the society is very good. However, the letter writers are arbitrarily attacking the previous employers in order to seek employment. The reporter does not investigate and publishes it at will, whether it is in line with the original intention of Mr. setting up this column. 2. The article said "There is a certain time limit even for going to the toilet." Has the reporter of your newspaper investigated and confirmed this kind of unfounded slander? This kind of harsh system is not only absent in our factory, but even prisons cannot implement it for prisoners. 3. There are nearly 3 million residents in Shanghai, and there is no day without layoffs. Now, a female worker with low skills who left the factory eight months ago is using your newspaper's valuable pages to make sensational remarks, hoping to win the sympathy of the society, and your newspaper is also willing to be used by her, which is deeply regrettable. I have always known and loved you, dare to send my humble sincerity, and I am extremely terrified to see the end of the film. I respectfully wish you peace and good health.

Yours sincerely, Nie Lusheng

Editor's note: The object of this magazine is the entire society, not any individual. Therefore, for contributions from all parties, as long as the content is substantial and related to the improvement of workers' lives, regardless of whether the contributor is the "employer" or "male and female workers", we are happy to publish it. Our only wish is to use this small publication as a mirror for society. Especially regarding the self-employment introduction column, we are not only standing in the position of a third party, strictly maintaining neutrality, not making judgments, and not taking sides; we fundamentally have no preconceived notions of right and wrong, but just give the unemployed an opportunity to shout. I am sincerely afraid of causing misunderstandings between the two parties, and I have to add a few words to clarify my attitude; I do not dare to say that I have any rebuttal to anyone or any aspect.

Special Self-Employment Introduction

My Worries 254

— Ke Zhong

I, who have an unfortunate destiny, no, I, in this turbulent, economically collapsing, and increasingly unemployed society, have just spent a lot of effort and relied on the help of friends to find a place to eat. I thought that "three meals a day and seven feet to sleep" would not have to worry for a year or half a year. Who knew that "the sky has unpredictable winds and clouds, and people have misfortunes in the morning and evening." Before completing a month of service, suddenly the order to "make a list and hand over" came down. Alas, this is no different from pouring a bucket of cold water on my back and hitting my rice bowl with a stick. Although the handover period has not yet arrived, my luggage will finally grow legs and move around soon - at the end of April. Following that, "three meals a day and seven feet of sleep" will all shoot like arrows at my cowardly soul for the sake of supporting "weak life"?

Of course, in the dead of night, when tossing and turning in bed, I keep thinking; even during the day, while working, I cannot but consider the future problems. Because the strange phenomenon in society is that bread is not there waiting for you to take it, let alone dream that it can reach your mouth. You must sharpen your head and use all your energy to grab it. But what is the use of using all your energy? Ordinary people have already got it first! Ordinary people borrowed the hands of others and took it in their own hands! Ordinary people relied on the strength of others to get it... Now, it is like "a patient competing with a strongman" to think that a cowardly person like me can use his fists and feet to compete with others for bread in this strange society. Isn't it ridiculous and pitiful? Sometimes I think it is better to commit suicide, but "suicide is a cowardly act, a useless person who cannot fight", "Heaven gave me talent, it must be useful", etc., ideas occupy my mind again. Because I am confident that although I am not a "perfect and omnipotent" youth, I have a superb will and will definitely have some achievements. Cowardly? Useless person? How can I be willing to accept it. Heaven gave me talent, it must be useful! However, my situation is like this, what is the use after all? These, these thoughts, like surging waves, are constantly rising and hitting in my mind!

Looking at the current situation is like this, recalling the past situation, I was just fighting in an environment of thorns and thorns, and the result is the current situation. Then, what will happen in the future? According to the public rule of "knowing the past, knowing the present, and inferring the future", I am not as good as before now, and of course the situation will get worse and worse in the future. Alas! What will happen in the future?·········

As for my skills, in addition to being proficient in the money industry, I also know a little about the oil and wine industry; I also know a little about writing, and I often publish articles in the supplements of the Wuxi National Herald and the Xi Bao. Also, I can write Wei inscriptions, and I can write more than a thousand characters per hour in pen, and I have a rough knowledge of English. I am now willing to work as an assistant editor or proofreader in a newspaper (I have experience), a bank or money shop employee, a company or school clerk or accountant, etc. Provide food and accommodation, salary is not counted. Correspondence address This publication will forward.

Movie Special

My Humble Opinion on The Sign of the Cross 256

— Si Ping

I believe that whether you are a Christian or a non-Christian, everyone who has seen The Sign of the Cross will have a very deep impression. Although it has a strong religious color, in terms of film and drama art, this film can be said to be a masterpiece of the great director Cecil B. DeMille, and it is also a rare masterpiece in the film industry for several years.

I have often asked myself why Christianity has been so powerful in European and American countries for thousands of years, and why the piety of European and American people who are so scientifically advanced has lasted for so long. Historians say that Western civilization is formed by the fusion of two elements: Christian doctrine and Greek scholarship. Cecil B. DeMille's The Sign of the Cross film maximizes this essence.

Religion is originally a personal matter, and it is also a part of social life. Cecil B. DeMille's film takes religion as its position, and other films take love or crime as their position. There is not much relationship in film art. Starting from this point of view to criticize The Sign of the Cross, Cecil B. DeMille's description of the conflict between non-religion and religion in the cultural history of Europe at that time is very profound. Rome at that time was the most powerful force representing the so-called The Pagan World. The greatness and barbarism of Rome met the intrusion of Jesus' spirit of universal love. In the plot of The Sign of the Cross, it is lined with interpolation very shocking. A group of men, women, old and young Christians are not subdued by power, singing hymns and bravely facing death calmly. The Roman Governor and the Roman Empress, who were so powerful and invincible, repeatedly tempted them unsuccessfully, but in the end they were conquered by the commoner Christian girl. The two embraced each other and were martyred, concealing the clues that Rome and even the whole of Europe were conquered by the power of Christianity later.

In general, The Sign of the Cross is a historical film that thoroughly depicts an important key to the transformation era of ancient Western civilization. As for other characteristics, I may have places that are not satisfactory due to my personal views or doctrines. Someone has criticized it before, and my intention is only to point out the main purpose of Cecil B. DeMille's direction of this film as I personally saw it. I also think that the translation of this film is very inappropriate.

Editor's note: Ling Hejun's and Si Pingjun's two reviews, one is from a non-Christian, and the other is from a Christian, but both have insightful views. Another thing in common is that they all think that the translation of this kind of film is inappropriate. However, the four words "Romance in the Palace" also have their advantages; the most obvious is an attempt to cover up the heavy religious color, in order to avoid the criticism of our general pagan or even Atheistic people. Or this attempt has other paths to success, so I would like to ask Ling He and Si Ping to try to propose one or two more solemn translations that are in line with the film. If appropriate, it will be published, but this point will never be discussed publicly. Not smart

Film Review

On the Silver Screen of the Nanjing Grand Theater 257

— Zhong

Yesterday's film change in Nanjing, although advertised with the names of stars Charlie Chaplin and Mitzi Green, was actually more like a short film festival, with a total of five films. The results were very good, as detailed below:

First was the Pathé News Special (Special Contribution), mostly about sports and aviation. There were many magnificent shots of airplanes lined up, which could inspire excitement in us who advocate for national salvation through aviation. Secondly, there was a short film about the customs of the Malay Archipelago. Although not long, it was quite interesting and offered a glimpse into the lives of people in the tropics. The cinematography was very artistic, resembling high-class landscape paintings, unlike the simplicity of ordinary ethnographic films.

Next was a cartoon slapstick film (Charcoal Drawing), which was unremarkable.

After the "Coming Attractions of the Treasures Fair" and the intermission, came "Little Orphan Annie."

The story is very short, telling of a little girl whose father is away on business. To help an orphan in an orphanage, she arranges for the orphan to be taken in by an old woman. She then goes to the old woman's house to play with the orphan. The orphan is unfortunately injured, and she takes care of him. On Christmas Eve, she attends the orphanage's celebration and discovers that the person dressed as Santa Claus is her father, who has returned from afar, and thus the family is reunited.

This is based on a long-running comic strip from an American newspaper. The script and organization are very good. The protagonist is Mitzi Green, and her performance naturally reveals innocence and humor. The most wonderful part is when she plays with the orphan, she dresses up as the "Marx Brothers" from "A Night at the Opera" in a humorous performance. She also plays a stubborn old woman, with meticulous portrayal. Her talent for imitation is undeniable. Buster Phelps, who plays the orphan, is only five or six years old, but his expressions are already remarkable. Every cry and every smile can win people's sympathy.

The other child actors are also good, and the adult supporting actors can only be considered as backdrops.

The sets are good. The lighting is a bit too dark in some places. The cinematography is excellent. For example, in the scene where the orphan falls from upstairs, the children in the audience show sympathy and laugh. There are no interjections. The whole film has laughter-inducing slapstick and anxiety-inducing tension. As such, it deserves to be called an "Excellent Work."

The ending of this film is immediately followed by the beginning of "Easy Street," a work by Charlie Chaplin from five or six years ago. Presumably, because Chaplin hasn't had any new works in the past two years, and the audience has been longing for him for a long time, the RKO company has revamped it, adding beautiful music to meet the need.

The story of the slapstick film is empty. It depicts Chaplin as a police officer who, fortunately, cleverly defeats a strongman, and is thus admired by the people. That's all there is to it in the three reels of film. There's nothing to say about the directing. The lighting, cinematography, sets, and makeup are all simple and immature, far below today's standards. But even though it is immature, the coherence and contrast are very good (half of the poor lighting, etc., is due to the fact that it's an old film being re-released). I haven't seen Chaplin's signature splayed-foot, coolly humorous attitude for five or six years (he has changed his style from "The Gold Rush," "The Kid," to "City Lights"). And I suspect this film may be a work from ten years ago (but I can't say for sure). Anyway, although this film is unreasonable, full of loopholes, and forced slapstick, it is ultimately not unbearable. A genius artist can still display his genius!

Of the five films, "Little Orphan Annie" is the longest and best. Although the music in "Easy Street" is very good, it's just average in comparison. In today's environment, it's just a mediocre work.

"Tianyi" Relocation News 258

"Dawn" Also Filmed

Recently, the Tianyi Film Company is planning to move because the open space near the film studio has been developed into a road. The noise of vehicles is constant, which is very detrimental to sound recording. A few days ago, Shao Zuiweng and Qiu Qixiang inspected the Lin Family Garden at the end of Baoshan Road in Zhabei. The location is quiet and sparsely populated, making it a good place for shooting sound films. However, the journey is too far, so they may look for another place. Therefore, a decision has not yet been made.

The script for little sister Liming Hui's second film has been titled "Dawn," which happens to be the same as her name. The script was written by her father, Li Jinhui. The theme of the script is to adopt realistic themes to give a painful cry for the working masses, and at the same time, to expose the oppressive and exploitative means of the propertied class. Qiu Qixiang has been discussing the breakdown of the script and filming ideas with the Li family for days. It is said that filming may begin around the 20th of this month.

Another Review of "The Sign of the Cross" 259

— Ming

Although "The Sign of the Cross" has been playing for four days, its greatness and success are indeed worth talking about again.

If we read ancient European history and look at the part that describes the Roman Empire, who can not feel emotional? Seeing the Christian Crusaders of the Renaissance, who can not be moved? But those orthodox histories are by no means as powerful or as grand as unofficial histories or films, and not as deeply touching. The greatness of director Cecil B. DeMille cannot be denied either. Which of "The Ten Commandments," "The King of Kings," "Forbidden Fruit," and "Volga Boatman" is not glorious? This time, "The Sign of the Cross" establishes DeMille's highest position. In fact, it is better to say that this is a religious film rather than a historical film, and it is better to say that it is an ethical film rather than a religious film. It has extremely profound meaning and extremely beautiful techniques, melting joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness into one furnace, integrating art, thought, ethics, and entertainment into one. How difficult is that? This film is Paramount's unprecedented achievement. In terms of technique alone, it has surpassed "Grand Hotel."

In fact, there are also considerable regrets in the story, but through the director's efforts, it does not affect the dignity or greatness of the whole film at all. Under such a great director, new records have also been created in all other technical aspects. The greatness of the set design and the purity of the lighting are worthy of praise and admiration.

He deliberately makes a startling stroke, which seems to be unrelated to the previous scene, but in the next scene, he immediately connects them with a vivid thread, seamlessly. In terms of cinematography, he never uses novel angles, but the result of the combination is very "beautiful" and solid.

In terms of actors, three of the five protagonists are "Frederic March, Elissa Landi, and Claudette Colbert," genius actors we have long recognized. The other two, Charles Laughton and Vivian Tobin, are new stars and are also exceptionally beautiful. The Boston Daily News commented: "…This is a great film that surpasses any blockbuster. Anyone in the world can appreciate it. Everyone should experience it…" This is indeed not an exaggeration.

Lee Tracy's Reasons for Not Getting Married 260

— Shichun

Lee Tracy is now advocating for not getting married. His reason is that once you have a wife, your life is surrounded by a layer of permanent iron fences and you can't be free. If you marry someone who is not in the film industry, she will definitely not want to live in Hollywood, and she will definitely not be at ease. Because in the film industry, except for old people in their fifties or sixties, someone will definitely fabricate all kinds of romances for you, and inevitably make your wife jealous. If you marry someone in the film industry, that is especially a lifetime of trouble. You have to obey her everywhere. I'm not saying I'll never get married, but the time I work in Hollywood is not the time to get married, because I believe that if you get married, you can't get divorced. I think it's better not to get married than to get married and then divorced.

Another Letter Proves Its "Existence" 261

— Huang Zhongqiang

Dear Editor:

I read Ling Hejun's reply to the article about the double-seat rickshaw in the "Madame Butterfly" film. Now I will describe what I know as follows:

In the past, there were two types of rickshaws in Japan. One type was wide and called "share-riding," which is the double-seat rickshaw seen in the Butterfly film. The other type was the ordinary one-person rickshaw called "single-riding." But now this kind of "share-riding" is rare. According to the current progress in Japan, perhaps in a few years, even the "single-riding" will no longer be seen. I read Ling Hejun's reply in this publication about the double-seat rickshaw in the "Madame Butterfly" film. Ling Hejun said that it certainly doesn't exist in Japan, and it seems that he also said that it has never existed since ancient times. I think it may not exist now, but it certainly existed in the past. If Ling Hejun doesn't believe it, he can ask older Japanese people or those who have studied in Japan for a longer period of time. Then you can understand the inside story. (With thanks)

Film Novel "Tarakanova" (5) 262

— Meihua

Unexpected things often happen. Orlov's disgrace with Catherine is just like Princess Tarakanova's being deceived by Orlov! Because when Orlov was sent to deceive Princess Tarakanova, Catherine could not bear the loneliness in the palace and fell in love with a young and handsome member of the royal family. At this time, Orlov in Catherine's mind was just an obedient subject, not a lovable person she could not be without for a moment.

Princess Tarakanova was bound and taken to the palace like a prisoner who had committed a serious crime. But she was very calm in her heart. She thought: "You are an adulterous woman who murdered her husband. I am the daughter of Queen Elizabeth. Why should I be afraid of you!"

Catherine originally wanted to behead her in a fit of rage, but when she saw her stubborn expression, she knew that she was just a naive and innocent daughter without any schemes. Such a person seemed to have no conspiracy. She must have been deceived by someone. So Catherine said to her: "If you are willing to remove the name of Princess Tarakanova and no longer have excessive delusions, I can let you go."

"What? You can kill me, but you can't take away my name as Princess Tarakanova." As she spoke, she widened her two round eyes, and a fire of desire shot out from those eyes, as if the magnificent furnishings and majestic guards in the palace were all under the command of Princess Tarakanova.

Catherine ordered her to be tied up in prison, stripped of her clothes, exposing her snow-white flesh, and whipped on that skin with a thick whip, one stroke at a time. She cried娇, she turned宛, she struggled, she was angry, she imagined that great figures in history must suffer some hardships. She could only endure the pain, thinking of her lovely and hateful Orlov.

Orlov, under the double oppression of conscience and nervous stimulation, felt extremely ashamed and regretful for Princess Tarakanova. He thought: "Let's commit suicide. But if I commit suicide, she will still be threatened with harsh beatings and live a miserable life. Moreover, besides myself, who else can save her?" When Orlov thought of this, he went to see Catherine again. She seemed to have not seen him for a few days and was still somewhat attached to him. Looking at Orlov's appearance and voice, he was still as moving as before. She unconsciously regained her enthusiasm for him. Orlov concealed his inner pain and accompanied Catherine to make merry, while secretly, because he had regained Catherine's favor and at the same time regained his original prestige, he faked Catherine's order to release Tarakanova, who was dreaming of being a princess. (To be continued)
